msg:The hotel we stayed in this time is a Zen culture theme hotel. The hotel environment is good and the location is superior. It only takes 800 meters to walk to the Leshan Giant Buddha, which takes about 10 minutes. The walking path outside the hotel is lined with trees on both sides, and it won't be too hot. If you don't want to walk, the hotel has a sightseeing bus to send you to the visitor center to take the scenic area sightseeing bus to the entrance of the Leshan Giant Buddha. You can also take the scenic area sightseeing bus back to the hotel. It is very convenient. The front desk service is enthusiastic. Each room has a butler. Our butler is Miss Xiao Guo. The service is very good and very thoughtful. We stayed for two nights. On the first night, we returned to the room and felt that the room had a little smell. After communicating with the butler Xiao Guo, We were immediately given a new room, which was very fast. We had originally planned to just forget about the first night and get another one the next day, but we didn't expect Miss Guo to change us to a room on the 2nd floor without a second thought. The room cleaning the next day was also very timely and efficient. The staff were very dedicated and could handle problems in a timely manner, putting themselves in the guests' shoes. The hotel has many Zen cultural activities, and it's also very good to practice Tai Chi in the morning. There are also Chinese-style yoga, Zen tea sharing in the tea room, flower arrangement activities, incense compilation activities, and copying of the Heart Sutra. There are really too many activities. I will stay at this hotel again next time, and I will recommend it to my friends and family. It was a very satisfying stay!

Green plants can be seen everywhere, and the air is filled with a faint fragrance of flowers. The room layout is reasonable and comfortable. The bedroom and bathroom are separated, and there is also a separate tea room for meditation. At the same time, the hotel has an antique Zen meditation room, which provides sutra copying services and displays the process of self-copying sutras. You can experience a different kind of peace of mind in this process. The room is cleaned in time, the items are of high quality, and the bathrobes and Zen clothes are soft and skin-friendly and comfortable to wear. The overall environment is very clean and tidy, providing a quiet and comfortable living experience.
The hotel's service is very thoughtful and considerate. The housekeeper Xiao Hou is enthusiastic and meticulous. He meets our needs in a timely manner, introduces the hotel facilities and Zen cultural activities in detail, and provides a comprehensive Leshan travel guide. Breakfast provides a rich variety of Leshan specialty snacks, which we can enjoy without going out, such as Bobo chicken, tofu brain, beef cakes, etc. There are also warm night snacks on weekends, allowing people to walk in the yard after dinner to achieve the process of mind and body healing. In general, the environment here is quiet and peaceful, and there are rich and diverse activities to participate in, which brings us a unique and comfortable experience.

In addition, as a pet-friendly hotel, all service staff including the cleaning lady are very friendly to dogs, which is rare. There is a large lawn outside the hotel for dogs to play freely. It is especially recommended for friends who have dogs at home.
